**Prior chunk:** `0090-pipeline-commitment-ux` **built + closed 2026-06-22** → [`closed/`](closed/0090-pipeline-commitment-ux/plan.md). **Parked:**
- **0085-a — `linkQuickbooksId` is accepted without verifying it matches the dealer's name in QBO** (Codex Medium, [eval](closed/0085-dealer-contact-dedup/eval-2026-06-19-1147.md)) — `createDealer`'s link-on-match born-links a new dealer to whatever `linkQuickbooksId` the re-submit carries; a forged hidden field could link to an arbitrary *unlinked* QB Customer (the `dealers_quickbooks_id` partial-unique index blocks already-linked ones), which the 0084 auto-push then *updates* with the dealer's data. **Admin-only, low probability** (Codex declined to frame it as privesc — single-tenant, admins can already create links through the UI). The `reuseContactId` twin was **fixed in-cycle** (`eba6126`); this half is deferred because validating an arbitrary Customer Id needs a QB read (`fetchCustomerById` + `DisplayName` compare) that conflicts with the best-effort principle (a QB outage shouldn't block a legit link). Fix shape: when QB is reachable, verify the matched Customer's `DisplayName` equals the dealer name before honoring the link; skip-and-create on a QB miss/outage. **Un-park trigger:** next hardening of the QBO link path, or a wrong-Customer-overwrite report.
- **0084-a — clearing a dealer's contact field in-app doesn't blank the QBO Customer field** (Codex Medium, [eval](closed/0084-dealer-create-qbo-customer/eval-2026-06-18-1851.md)) — `mapDealerToCustomer` only sets `GivenName`/`FamilyName`/`PrimaryEmailAddr`/`PrimaryPhone` when truthy, and the QBO update is `sparse:true`, so *clearing* email/phone/contact-name/address in the app (now auto-propagated by 0084's `updateDealer` push) leaves the old value in QuickBooks. **Not a regression** — the omit-on-empty mapper shape predates 0084 (0070); the common *change-to-a-new-value* case propagates fine. Same family as **0070 follow-up (c)**. Fix shape: in the *update* branch send the QBO sparse-clear representation for app-empty fields (verify the API shape for blanking `PrimaryEmailAddr`/`GivenName`); keep *create* omitting empties. **Un-park trigger:** owner wants in-app field clears to propagate to QBO, or next hardening of the push path.
- **0084-b — best-effort QBO push is awaited inline, adding QBO latency to the dealer-save response** (Codex Low, same eval) — `autoPushActiveDealerToQuickbooks` awaits token-refresh + QBO fetch/create/update + backfill before the action returns `{ ok: true }`, so a slow QuickBooks makes "Save dealer" feel slow (errors are still swallowed; rollback is correct). **Consistent with the 0077 calendar best-effort pattern** (also awaited inline). Fix shape: a durable background/outbox job, or a tight timeout around the push. **Un-park trigger:** a slow-save report, or moving the calendar/QBO best-effort side-effects onto an outbox.
- **0082-a — `sendMsaEnvelope` concurrent double-send** (Codex High, pre-existing — [eval](closed/0082-quote-msa-decouple/eval-2026-06-15-1945.md)) · the external BoldSign `sendSignatureRequest` call precedes the guarded `provider_document_id` persist, so two concurrent callers can post two envelopes (only one id saved; the orphan's signed-webhook 404s). Predates 0082 (the decouple didn't touch the ordering); after the eval's admin-only retighten it fires from an admin confirm dialog that disables while pending — low probability. Fix shape: reserve a send slot in the DB (or row/advisory lock) before calling BoldSign. **Un-park trigger:** an orphaned-envelope report, or the next hardening of the MSA send path.
- **danger-callout component (≈0082, follow-up to 0081)** · the app has no shared inline danger/warning callout (the pink box + red icon badge + heading + subtext from the 0081 owner inspiration image) and has ~8 duplicated ad-hoc red error panels (`border-red-200 bg-red-50 text-red-800`-style) across login / quotes / msa / quickbooks. A shared `Callout color="red"` would unify them and host the soft-red destructive action. **Scoped out of 0081** (owner: "button only now" 2026-06-15). Un-park trigger: 0081 ships, or the next time a destructive/error panel needs touching.
- **0078 follow-up (a): in-flight upload can be omitted from the sent email but persist on the sent quote** (Codex High, [eval](closed/0078-quote-attachments/eval-2026-06-12-2043.md)) — a slow `uploadQuoteAttachment` racing a direct `sendQuote` call: the send snapshots attachments before the upload's insert, emails PDF-only, then the row lands on the now-`sent` quote. **Mitigated:** the dialog disables Send while uploading, and a re-send includes the persisted file (self-healing) — reachable only by bypassing the UI. Fix shape: re-read attachments inside/after the guarded transition, or bump `quotes.updatedAt` on attachment insert so the send optimistic-lock covers it. **Un-park trigger:** a report of a persisted-but-unsent attachment, or next hardening of the send path.
- **0078 follow-up (b): attachment changes not covered by the send optimistic lock** (Codex Medium, same eval) — removing an attachment between `sendQuote`'s snapshot and its guarded UPDATE can still email the removed doc; the lock only checks `quotes.updatedAt`. Same UI gate + narrow race as (a). Fix shape: same as (a) — make attachment mutations bump `quotes.updatedAt`. **Un-park trigger:** with (a).
- **0078 follow-up (c): parallel uploads can bypass the 20 MB total cap** (Codex Medium, same eval) — the upload cap check is read-then-write without a quote lock, so concurrent direct uploads each see `existingTotal=0`. The send-time guard still fails closed (nothing over-size goes out); only DB/GCS growth is unbounded. UI uploads sequentially. Fix shape: do the cap check + insert in a `quotes`-row-locked transaction. **Un-park trigger:** an over-cap storage report, or a prod arming of the feature.
- **0078 follow-up (d): server MIME validation trusts caller `File.type` only** (Codex Medium, same eval) — no extension/magic-byte check; the same value is stored + emailed as `contentType`. The file is emailed (not executed/served) and the uploader is a trusted authenticated coach, so it's a defensible v1 limit. Fix shape: sniff magic bytes (or validate extension↔MIME) before `putObject`. **Un-park trigger:** a malformed-attachment report, or before opening upload to a less-trusted role.
- **0078 follow-up (e): GCS object orphaned if the DB insert throws after `putObject`** (Codex Low, same eval) — the upload writes to GCS before inserting the row, with no compensating delete on insert failure. Retention is keep-forever anyway (orphan = harmless storage); `recordAudit` is best-effort (never throws). Fix shape: wrap insert in try/catch → best-effort `deleteObject` on failure. **Un-park trigger:** an orphaned-object report, or next hardening of the upload path.
- ~~**0077 follow-up (a): reconcile always sends `sendUpdates='all'` — non-prod envs would email real invites**~~ — **RESOLVED 2026-06-12** (`9277f60`): added `calendarSendUpdates()` (mirrors boldsign's `isProductionEnv`) — `sendUpdates='all'` only when `APP_ENV==='production'`, else `'none'`, threaded through every reconcile create/patch/delete call. The projection still runs in non-prod (events created/patched/deleted) but guests aren't emailed. Integration tests assert both env branches. So non-prod is now safe to arm. (Surfaced by the 2026-06-12 live smoke, not Codex.) **Live keyless+DWD round-trip PASSED 2026-06-12** (organizer = calendar displayName "EventPro" — the owner's chosen brand, no rename).
- **0076 follow-up (a): `loadTaxMappingAdmin` collapses a QBO error to "disconnected"** (Codex Low, [eval](closed/0076-quickbooks-tax-code-mapping/eval-2026-06-11-1014.md)) — any QBO/token/fetch failure falls back to the read-only "Connect QuickBooks" view even when a connection exists but QBO errored, hiding drift/broken-link diagnostics + misdirecting remediation. The fallback is **safe** (the rest of `/admin/lookups` stays up). Fix shape: a distinct `connected: true, error: string` state rendering "Couldn't load QuickBooks tax codes" while keeping local rows visible. **Un-park trigger:** a transient-QBO-error report on the mapping page.
- **0076 follow-up (b): `refreshTaxRates` reports planned writes, not rows actually updated** (Codex Low, same eval) — the action returns `updated: writes.length`, but the compare-and-set `.where()` can legitimately match 0 rows when a province was concurrently re-mapped → the toast count overcounts. DB state stays correct (the CAS correctly skips the stale write); only the reported number is optimistic. Fix shape: count `.returning()` rows from each CAS update and report that. **Un-park trigger:** next touch of the refresh path, or a wrong-count report.
- **0075 follow-up (a): compact/decorated QB tax-code names miss the name match** (Codex Low — speculative, [eval](closed/0075-quickbooks-tax-rate-source/eval-2026-06-10-1557.md)) — the matcher anchors the province code to the trailing whitespace token ("HST ON" → ON) + the full name, so non-standard names like "HSTON", "PEI", or "HST ON (13%)" fall through to **unmatched/flagged** (keeps the app rate — fail-safe, by design). Fix shape: the deferred per-province manual override (decision 3) resolves these; or broaden the heuristic if a real company uses such names. **Un-park trigger:** a real connected company has a province-naming code the trailing-token heuristic misses.
- **0074 follow-up (a): stale tax code on a taxed→untaxed Estimate re-push** (Codex Medium, [eval](closed/0074-quickbooks-tax-alignment/eval-2026-06-10-1259.md)) — `mapQuoteToEstimate` omits `TxnTaxDetail` when a quote is untaxed, but `updateEstimate` always sends `sparse:true`, so a re-push of a now-untaxed quote onto an Estimate that already has a `TxnTaxCodeRef` can leave the old code → QBO keeps taxing. Rare transition; create + taxed-update paths are correct. Fix shape: on an untaxed update, explicitly clear the Estimate's tax (full update, or the right `TxnTaxDetail`/`GlobalTaxCalculation` to zero it) — verify the clear mechanism on the CA sandbox. **Un-park with the live CA Estimate-with-tax smoke.**
- ~~**0073 follow-up (a): sparse-update line semantics**~~ — **RESOLVED 2026-06-10** by the live re-push smoke: QBO's sparse `updateEstimate` replaces the `Line` collection correctly (Estimate #1001 stayed 2 lines on re-push, SyncToken read-before-write held). See [eval addendum](closed/0073-quote-estimate-push/eval-2026-06-10-0911.md). Residual minor (test-infra): the DB integration suite flakes under default parallelism on the sandbox session-pooler 15-client cap (4 DB test files + dev server) — run serially (`vitest --no-file-parallelism`) or point integration tests at the direct connection. **Un-park:** if test flakiness becomes annoying.
- **0071 follow-up (a): partial multi-page item read can destructively sync** (Codex High residual, [eval](closed/0071-quickbooks-item-pull/eval-2026-06-09-1429.md)) — `fetchItems` stops at the first short page, so a transient HTTP-200 empty *later* page (page 1 full, page 2 silently empty) returns an incomplete-but-non-empty set; the pull then archives the "missing" linked rows + purges. The in-cycle zero-syncable guard (`7f86715`) covers the empty / all-non-syncable cases but **not** this partial-multi-page case. Fix shape: validate `fetchItems` pagination (detect an unexpectedly-short later page / use QBO `totalCount`) and/or a "this pull would archive+purge most of the linked catalog → require explicit confirm" threshold. **Un-park trigger: before enabling a prod item pull** (sandbox-only + admin-initiated today).
- **0070 follow-up (a): linked double-submit stale `SyncToken` 400** (Codex Medium, [eval](closed/0070-quickbooks-dealer-push/eval-2026-06-09-1211.md)) — two concurrent pushes of the same *linked* dealer both read token N; the first rotates QBO to N+1, the second posts N → stale-object 400. Read-before-write narrows but doesn't close the window; rare for on-demand single-admin use. Fix shape: catch the stale-token error from `updateCustomer`, re-fetch the SyncToken, retry once. **Un-park trigger:** a concurrent-push report, or next hardening of the push path.
- **0070 follow-up (b): create-before-guard orphan QBO Customer + misleading `created` report on a lost race** (Codex Medium, same eval) — the QBO Customer is created before the `quickbooks_id IS NULL` backfill guard; if a concurrent push/sync links the dealer in between, the new Customer is orphaned (no local link) yet the call still returns `created`. Orphan-on-lost-race is by-design per intent; the misleading report is the new nuance. Fix shape: inspect `.returning()`; on zero rows report non-`created` + optionally deactivate the orphan QBO Customer. **Un-park trigger:** an orphaned-customer report, or next hardening of the push path.
- **0070 follow-up (c): sparse update can't clear fields removed in-app** (Codex Medium, same eval) — clearing a dealer's address/province/email/phone locally won't clear it in QBO (a sparse update leaves omitted fields as-is). Defensible for a "push to populate" v1; whether the app should wipe QBO fields is a **product decision**. Fix shape: send QBO clear-semantics for null/empty locals on update + clearing tests. **Un-park trigger:** owner wants in-app field clears to propagate to QBO.
- **0070 follow-up (d): missing `SyncToken` guessed as `'0'`** (Codex Low, same eval) — `current.SyncToken ?? '0'` guesses if a Customer read omits the token (hypothetical — QBO always returns it). Fix shape: throw when `current.SyncToken == null` rather than guessing. **Un-park trigger:** any stale-token 400 noise on update.
- **0070 follow-up (e): duplicate-name detection only matches string `code: "6240"`** (Codex Low, same eval) — `e.code === '6240'` could miss a numeric code; the `/\b6240\b/` text regex runs only on JSON-parse failure. QBO returns string Fault codes today. Fix shape: `String(e.code) === '6240'` (+ scan Fault `Detail`). **Un-park trigger:** a duplicate-name push surfacing as a generic 500 instead of the friendly path.
- **0069 follow-up (a): duplicate-`create` for two QB customers sharing name+address** (Codex Medium, [eval](closed/0069-quickbooks-dealer-sync/eval-2026-06-08-1703.md)) — two QBO customers with identical `lower(name)+lower(address)` and no existing dealer both insert (distinct QB IDs → no conflict), creating duplicate dealers. **By-design today** per intent ("we don't try to be clever about near-duplicates"); rare (QBO IDs unique). Fix shape: track an in-memory name+address set during apply, collapse later same-key customers to `skip`. **Un-park trigger:** real QBO data produces same-name+address dupes, or a prod sync is enabled.
- **0069 follow-up (b): name-only match when both addresses are empty** (Codex Medium, same eval) — `nameAddrKey` normalizes a null address to `''`, so an address-less dealer links to an address-less same-name QB customer (name-only match). **Inherited from the 0060 importer's `lower(coalesce(address,''))` semantics** — not a new regression. Fix shape: require a non-blank formatted address on both sides before `link` (else `create` / manual-review). **Un-park trigger:** enabling a prod sync where address-less dealers exist, or a wrong-link report.
- **0069 follow-up (c): duplicate *existing* dealers → nondeterministic link/collision** (Codex Medium, same eval) — `classifyDealerSyncPlan`'s `byNameAddr` map is last-wins; if two existing dealers share name+address (one linked to a different QB ID, one unlinked), a customer can `link` to the unlinked one instead of `skip-collision`. Requires a rare DB state (the unique index is on `quickbooks_id`, not name+address). Fix shape: store arrays per key; `skip-collision` if any same-key dealer holds a different QB ID; skip-ambiguous if multiple unlinked match. **Un-park trigger:** next touch of the classifier, or a duplicate-dealer collision report.
- **0069 follow-up (d): archived dealers participate in sync matching** (Codex Medium, same eval) — `loadExistingDealers` reads all dealers (no `archivedAt IS NULL` filter) and the guarded link update doesn't exclude archived rows, so an archived dealer can be silently linked while the rest of the app excludes it. **Inherited from 0060** (also unfiltered). Fix shape: decide skip / revive / create-new for an archived name+address match, then filter `loadExistingDealers` + the update accordingly. **Un-park trigger:** archived dealers exist in a synced company, or the prod sync is enabled.

- **0065 follow-up (a): rate-snapshot TOCTOU** (Codex Medium from [`closed/0065-dealer-province-tax/eval-2026-06-04-1631.md`](closed/0065-dealer-province-tax/eval-2026-06-04-1631.md)) — `dealerTaxRatePct` reads the dealer's province→rate on the **app pool** before/outside the quote tx's `FOR UPDATE` dealer lock, so a concurrent `updateDealer` province change can snapshot a stale `tax_pct` onto a now-different-province quote. **Low-probability + self-healing** (next picker save / send re-derives). Fix shape: read the rate **inside** the quote tx from the `FOR UPDATE`-locked dealer's province. **Un-park trigger:** next touch of the quote write path, or any report of a wrong tax rate on a quote.

- 0061 follow-up (a): **`sendMsaEnvelope` links the quote AFTER the external BoldSign post** (Codex High from [`closed/0061-move-msa-action-to-quote/eval-2026-05-29-1418.md`](closed/0061-move-msa-action-to-quote/eval-2026-05-29-1418.md)) — the `quotes.msa_id` link UPDATE (`src/features/msa/actions.ts:383`) runs after `sendSignatureRequest` and ignores its result, so if the quote changes status (or is linked by another path) between preload and link, BoldSign holds a valid envelope but `acceptBundledQuote` later finds no row → the signed MSA activates while the bundled quote never auto-accepts. **Pre-existing** — predates 0061 (which only widened the guard draft→draft|sent); same family as **0041 follow-up (a)** (concurrent-send race). Fix shape: guarded `UPDATE … RETURNING` (`draft|sent` + `msa_id IS NULL`) BEFORE rendering/upload/BoldSign, abort if no row claimed. Un-park trigger: hardening the MSA send path, or any report of a signed-but-not-accepted bundled quote.
- 0059 follow-up (a): **`msa:edit` capability-pairing gap** (surfaced during 0059's eval, pre-existing) — `pnpm check:capability-pairing` reports `msa:edit` as server-gated (`src/features/msa/actions.ts:120,189`) with no UI affordance (`<Can capability="msa:edit">` / `useCan('msa:edit')`) pointing at it. Predates 0059 (confirmed against baseline). Fix shape: add a `<Can>`/`useCan('msa:edit')` to the MSA send affordance, OR add `// expected: server-only` to the action lines if the MSA send button is gated some other way. Un-park trigger: next touch of the MSA send UI, or a CI gate on `check:capability-pairing`.
- 0051 follow-up (a): **`constantTimeEquals` UTF-8 byte-length check** (Codex Low from [`closed/0051-dropbox-sign-to-boldsign/eval-2026-05-15-1644.md`](closed/0051-dropbox-sign-to-boldsign/eval-2026-05-15-1644.md)) — `src/lib/boldsign/webhook-verify.ts:52` compares JavaScript string length (UTF-16 code units) before calling `timingSafeEqual(Buffer.from(..., 'utf8'))`. A 64-char non-ASCII signature candidate has the same string length as the hex digest but a longer UTF-8 byte length, so `timingSafeEqual` throws instead of returning the 401 verification error. No signature bypass — malformed-input handling / availability. Fix shape: compare `Buffer.byteLength(a, 'utf8') !== Buffer.byteLength(b, 'utf8')` before `timingSafeEqual`. Un-park trigger: any sign of malformed-header production noise, or natural pickup when next touching `webhook-verify.ts`.
- 0051 follow-up (b): **Plan-doc grep-gate hygiene** (Codex Low from [`closed/0051-dropbox-sign-to-boldsign/eval-2026-05-15-1644.md`](closed/0051-dropbox-sign-to-boldsign/eval-2026-05-15-1644.md)) — Phase 7's "zero `dropbox` references in `src/`" claim is contradicted by two intentional exceptions: `.env.example:53` chunk-slug comment and `src/features/msa/template-version.ts:11` historical comment. Cosmetic chunk-doc only. Fix shape: refine the grep claim to acknowledge the two intentional exceptions, or rephrase the comments to non-grep-matchable spellings.
- 0050 follow-up (a): **TokenPill surrogate-pair truncation** (Codex Low from [`closed/0050-grid-pattern-resend/eval-2026-05-14-1059.md`](closed/0050-grid-pattern-resend/eval-2026-05-14-1059.md)) — `src/components/ui/token-pill.tsx:30`'s `value.slice(0, maxChars)` truncates by UTF-16 code units; a future caller passing a non-ASCII opaque value with an astral character on the boundary would split mid-surrogate and render a replacement character. No consumer today (the primitive landed ahead of any opaque-id surface). Fix shape: switch to code-point-aware slicing via `Array.from(value).slice(0, maxChars).join('')` or `Intl.Segmenter`. Un-park trigger: first surface adopts `<TokenPill>` with a non-ASCII value path.
- 0048 follow-up (a): **DST fall-back collision in `quoteDisplayName`** (Codex Low from [`closed/0048-quote-timestamp-naming/eval-2026-05-14-0859.md`](closed/0048-quote-timestamp-naming/eval-2026-05-14-0859.md)) — `src/features/quotes/display-name.ts` produces the same `quote-YYYYMMDD-HHmm` for two distinct UTC instants an hour apart during the autumn DST fall-back window (e.g. `2026-11-01T05:30:00Z` and `2026-11-01T06:30:00Z` both render as `quote-20261101-0130` in America/Toronto); `quoteDownloadFilename` likewise collides. Server-side persistence (GCS path `quotes/{quoteId}/{revision}.pdf` — id-keyed) is unaffected; collision is presentation-only and lasts one hour per year. Fix shape options: (i) include seconds in the display name (`quote-YYYYMMDD-HHmmss`); (ii) include a short id-tail suffix (`quote-…-<id-tail>`); (iii) emit the local-time offset to disambiguate (`quote-…-0400` vs `-0500`). Un-park trigger: a coach/customer reports two quotes sharing a display name in the November fall-back window, OR the next chunk that touches quote-identity display.
- 0049 follow-up (a): **Tabs rebuild on Headless UI `<TabGroup>`** (Codex Medium from [`closed/0049-migrate-to-catalyst/eval-2026-05-13-2316.md`](closed/0049-migrate-to-catalyst/eval-2026-05-13-2316.md)) — Phase 4d's custom `src/components/catalyst/tabs.tsx` is context-based and lacks the WAI-ARIA tabs contract: no Arrow/Home/End keyboard navigation, no `aria-controls`/`aria-labelledby` panel↔tab linkage, panels not connected to tabs by id. One callsite: `src/features/reports/reports-tabs.tsx`. Fix shape: replace the context-based implementation with Headless UI `<TabGroup>`/`<TabList>`/`<Tab>`/`<TabPanels>`/`<TabPanel>` wrapped to preserve the existing value-based `value`/`onValueChange` API (TabGroup is index-based natively, so a wrapper bridge is needed). Un-park trigger: any user complaint about `/reports` keyboard nav, OR natural pickup when scaffolding the next accessibility chunk.
- ~~0043 follow-up (a): **Composer-actions lift**~~ — shipped in-cycle on the 0043 feature branch at `5b63693` after user pushback ("action buttons are still on the bottom of the page"). Composer actions moved into a sticky toolbar at `top-16` inside the composer body (sits OUTSIDE the disabled fieldset so Preview/Close stay clickable on read-only quotes); `sticky` removed from the page-level `<PageHeader>` on `/quotes/new` + `/quotes/[id]` so the toolbar parks alone under the 64px `AppHeader` without double-stacking. Same commit batch also addressed user pushback on the `/quotes` row label (`View` → `Edit`, commit `57f3c17`) — the destination IS the composer, so the label should describe the operation, not the surface type; `docs/wiki/layout.md` View-xor-Edit rule refined accordingly.
- 0043 follow-up (b): **Row-action sweep into non-`*-columns.tsx` surfaces** (Codex Medium from [`closed/0043-portal-shell-conventions/eval-2026-05-13-1730.md`](closed/0043-portal-shell-conventions/eval-2026-05-13-1730.md)) — three callsites still render hand-rolled per-row actions outside the lint rule's path scope: the nested Quotes table on `/dealerships/[id]:225`, `src/features/services/services-admin.tsx:132`, `src/features/schedule/availability-admin.tsx:191`. Fix shape: port these to `<RowActions>` (preferred — same vocabulary win), or widen the lint rule's `files` glob to cover them.
- 0043 follow-up (c): **Status-pill sweep into calendar/people** (Codex Medium from [`closed/0043-portal-shell-conventions/eval-2026-05-13-1730.md`](closed/0043-portal-shell-conventions/eval-2026-05-13-1730.md)) — `src/app/(app)/calendar/event-detail.tsx:106,204` still renders campaign status via local `statusBadgeClass()`; `src/features/people/people-columns.tsx:169` renders lifecycle status with a hand-rolled rounded span. Fix shape: add `<CampaignStatusBadge status>` raw-enum variant + `<PersonLifecycleBadge>`, replace the inline chrome.
- 0043 follow-up (d): **Retire `STATUS_PILL_CLS`** (Codex Low from [`closed/0043-portal-shell-conventions/eval-2026-05-13-1730.md`](closed/0043-portal-shell-conventions/eval-2026-05-13-1730.md)) — `src/features/quotes/status-display.ts:13`'s map is no longer used by any swept callsite but is still exported + tested. Fix shape: delete `STATUS_PILL_CLS` + its test block, leaving `displayStatusKey()` as the shared helper.
- 0043 follow-up (e): **Lint vocabulary parity with labels map** (Codex Low from [`closed/0043-portal-shell-conventions/eval-2026-05-13-1730.md`](closed/0043-portal-shell-conventions/eval-2026-05-13-1730.md)) — `eslint-plugins/no-inline-row-action-label.mjs:20`'s `FORBIDDEN` set omits `Quote` even though `ROW_ACTION_LABELS.quote = 'Quote'`. Fix shape: derive the forbidden set from the label map directly (single source) or add `Quote` to the static set + RuleTester coverage.
- 0046 follow-up (a): **Outbox-style degraded-send retry** (Codex High from [`closed/0046-quote-mutable-after-send/eval-2026-05-13-1636.md`](closed/0046-quote-mutable-after-send/eval-2026-05-13-1636.md)) — when `sendQuote`'s guarded UPDATE commits but the subsequent GCS overwrite or email send fails, `sent_at` (and the derived validity window) has advanced without a delivered PDF / audit row; a manual Re-send recovers but a phantom-fresh validity window can mislead `acceptQuote` in the interim. Fix shape: introduce an `outbox` / `send_state` flag (`delivered | pending_pdf | pending_email`) that gates `acceptQuote` until delivery is confirmed, or hold the `sent_at` advance until both side effects succeed. Same family as the pre-0026 degraded-send retry gap (closed/0041 follow-up (a) covers the related concurrent-send race). Un-park trigger: shipping it now reduces a quiet-state risk; otherwise revisit when adding admin repair surfaces.
- 0046 follow-up (b): **ConfirmSendDialog hydration drift hypothesis** (Codex Low from [`closed/0046-quote-mutable-after-send/eval-2026-05-13-1636.md`](closed/0046-quote-mutable-after-send/eval-2026-05-13-1636.md)) — `formatValidUntil` runs `new Date(Date.now() + …)` in the dialog body while `open={false}`. Codex couldn't verify whether Base UI mounts hidden dialog content during SSR; practical risk is low (Radix unmounts hidden dialogs by default). Fix shape: compute the new validity date on dialog open via `useState`/`useEffect` rather than every render. Un-park trigger: a hydration warning surfaces in dev console for this dialog.
- 0044 follow-up (a): **MSA bundled-quote validity-deadline mismatch** (Codex Medium from [`closed/0044-quote-expiry-enforcement/eval-2026-05-13-1116.md`](closed/0044-quote-expiry-enforcement/eval-2026-05-13-1116.md)) — `sendMsaEnvelope` (`src/features/msa/actions.ts:285-292`) renders the bundled draft quote with `validUntilDate = today + quoteValidDays`, but the later `sendQuote` flip re-renders from a fresh `sentAt`, so the external MSA envelope PDF and the eventual sent quote PDF can disagree on "Valid until". Out of 0044's stated scope (closed/0041 owns the MSA bundle flow). Fix shape: persist a `quote_issued_at` timestamp the bundle and the send both read from, OR flip the bundled quote's lifecycle to `sent` inside the MSA envelope flow (which would also need to address MSA-vs-Quote acceptance ordering — closed/0041 deferred that to a separate "concurrent MSA+Quote send" follow-up).
- 0044 follow-up (b): **Expired filter pill on `/quotes`** (Codex Low from [`closed/0044-quote-expiry-enforcement/eval-2026-05-13-1116.md`](closed/0044-quote-expiry-enforcement/eval-2026-05-13-1116.md)) — expired quotes show the amber "expired" pill but still live under the "Sent" filter bucket (since the underlying row is `status='sent'`). Adding a dedicated Expired filter pill makes more sense if/when Option A (full enum + sweep) is promoted, since Option B's derived state can't be filtered server-side without re-fetching every row. Today the pill shows but the filter counts/pills don't separate expired from sent.
- 0045 follow-up (a): **`createPerson` / `updatePerson` appAccess + empty-email guard scope-creep** (Codex Medium from [`closed/0045-form-schema-as-contract/eval-2026-05-13-0937.md`](closed/0045-form-schema-as-contract/eval-2026-05-13-0937.md)) — `src/features/people/actions.ts:560` only enforces "email required when granting app access" on the `current.userId == null` (off→on) branch; an admin re-submitting `appAccess=1` with `email=''` against an already-linked person bypasses the guard, then `swapPrimaryIdentifier(..., '')` archives the primary email identifier while the auth-side sign-in email is preserved. Pre-existing bug, surfaced during 0045's eval but predates the chunk. Fix shape: hoist the email-required check out of the `userId == null` conditional so it fires on every appAccess=1 path, OR refuse `email=''` at the schema layer when `appAccess === '1'` (cross-field `.superRefine` on `personFormSchema`).
- 0045 follow-up (b): **`safeparse-required` ESLint rule policy hardening** (Codex Medium from [`closed/0045-form-schema-as-contract/eval-2026-05-13-0937.md`](closed/0045-form-schema-as-contract/eval-2026-05-13-0937.md)) — the rule accepts any reachable `safeParse` call regardless of (i) whether the argument is `Object.fromEntries(formData)`, (ii) whether it runs before mutation, or (iii) whether it sits in a dead branch. An adversarial action could insert/update from raw `formData`, then call `someSchema.safeParse({})` later and pass lint. Fix shape: tighten `eslint-plugins/safeparse-required.mjs` to assert the safeParse argument starts with `Object.fromEntries(...)` AND no mutation call (`db.update`/`db.insert`/`db.delete`) appears before the first `safeParse` in the action body. Adds RuleTester test coverage at the same time.
- 0041 follow-ups (deferred from chunk-end eval 2026-05-12 — see [`closed/0041-msa-send-bundled-envelope/eval-2026-05-12-2229.md`](closed/0041-msa-send-bundled-envelope/eval-2026-05-12-2229.md)): (a) **concurrent-send race on `sendMsaEnvelope`** (Codex High) — two callers can both post envelopes before the DB-claim lands; loser's webhook has no MSA row to correlate to. Fix shape: claim the send before external side effects (a `send_attempted_at` schema add + guarded UPDATE, or per-MSA advisory lock); paired naturally with (c) below; (b) **shared env-normalize helper** (Codex Medium) — `dropbox-sign/client.ts:83` uses raw `process.env.APP_ENV !== 'production'` while `email/send.ts` trims+lowercases; could test-mode a production deploy and still flip MSA rows to `active`; (c) **resend-envelope button** on the pending-MSA panel state (Codex Medium) — when `pending && !dropboxSignDocumentId`, the existing-MSA guard refuses a second `createMsaDraft` but `sendMsaEnvelope` is already idempotent — just needs UI; pairs naturally with (a); (d) **coach-scoped first-draft-Quote picker** (Codex Medium) — `firstDraftQuoteIdForDealer` is dealer-scoped, could pick another coach's draft in multi-coach dealers; better solved by an explicit Quote-picker UI than a `createdById` filter; (e) ~~**live BoldSign sandbox smoke**~~ **✅ RESOLVED 2026-05-22** (during 0055 close-out) — full envelope-post + webhook-signed round-trip exercised on Cloud Run (MSA #7→active, quote #3→accepted, signed PDF in GCS). The 0051 Codex Medium is answered: BoldSign does **not** need auto-detect — it accepts explicitly-placed `Initial`/`Signature` FormFields with `bounds`; the catch was a coordinate-units bug (BoldSign uses 96-DPI px, fixed by the `96/72` scale in `d06082b`), not field detection. (a)–(d) remain open.
- 0033 follow-up (carry-forward): retire hand-rolled validators (`parseId`/`field`/`parseLookupLabel`/`parseCampaignInput`/`validateContactInputs`) by writing per-action Zod schemas; replaces the `formDataSchema = z.instanceof(FormData)` passthrough; revisit when 0016 booking-intake lands so the public-facing form drives the schema-first conversion. **Superseded 2026-05-13 by `0045-form-schema-as-contract`** — covers the same retirement (Phase 7) plus the broader schema-sharing doctrine across all forms.

Eval report at `closed/0035-quote-composer/eval-2026-05-12-1650.md`. **Two follow-up commits** (`7366bbd` then `87022c6`) shipped after the close-the-chunk commit landed, on a different bug surfaced during the live send: stranded quote #1 hit the "Quote cannot be sent from status 'draft'" fallthrough because the atomic UPDATE's `eq(quotes.updatedAt, draft.updatedAt)` compared a microsecond-precision Postgres `timestamptz` against a millisecond-precision JS Date roundtrip — only matters when the row's `updated_at` was written by non-Drizzle SQL (e.g. `now()` in a one-off `UPDATE` to un-strand a previous degraded send). Fix: `date_trunc('milliseconds', updated_at) = $1::timestamptz` with explicit `.toISOString()` binding because drizzle's `sql\`\`` template doesn't propagate column-type metadata to bound JS Dates (postgres-js throws `ERR_INVALID_ARG_TYPE`). The original separate-issue trap that *caused* the strand: `GCS_CREDENTIALS_JSON` in `.env.local` was a **file path** but `gcs.ts:39-46` only handles inline JSON; `JSON.parse(path)` throws → `putObject` returns `{ error: 'GCS_CREDENTIALS_JSON is not valid JSON.' }` → `sendQuote` returns the "Quote sent but PDF upload failed; admin repair required" degraded path after the UPDATE already flipped status to `sent`. User-side fix: rename env to `GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=/path` (ADC fallback at `gcs.ts:37-49` picks it up, no code change); restart `pnpm dev` to clear the module-level cached `Storage` client (`gcs.ts:22`). Live verification: real send to `shannon@salesability.ca` dev-redirected to `david.hogan@networknode.ca` with subject prefix `[DEV→…]`, Resend `emailId 28a24ca4-2ec8-440e-8978-a758ff00567e`, PDF at `quotes/1/1.pdf` in `event-pro` bucket, `quote.sent` audit emitted. Eval reports inside the moved folder kept their historical `docs/chunks/0035-quote-composer/...` Plan headers (snapshot convention). Active sub-plan is now **None** — sequence forward is 0026 follow-ups (a–d) → 0025 7.2/7.3/7.4. Two new feedback memories worth saving: (i) Drizzle `sql\`\`` template doesn't propagate column-type metadata to bound JS Dates → pass `.toISOString()` + explicit `::timestamptz` cast; (ii) `<fieldset disabled>` cascades through descendant `<button>`s — pull always-enabled buttons outside the fieldset.

- **2026-05-11** — Scaffolded `0037-commercial-spine-msa/plan.md` and added to Parked **ahead of 0026/0035** as a prerequisite to 0026 Phase 2 unparking. Surfaced from a sales-funnel discussion that worked upstream from the existing 0026/0035 plans: user asked "shouldn't a quote move to an order which then creates a campaign?" Schema inspection confirmed `campaigns` was carrying double-duty commercial+operational columns (`fee`, `travel`, `depositPct`, `taxPct`, `quoteValidDays`, `salesLeadSourceId`) on what should be a pure delivery record. User then supplied the full Salesability MSA text, which resolved the question definitively — §1.iii: *"Each Quote issued by Salesability and accepted by the Client shall constitute a separate distinct and independent agreement and contractual obligation of the Parties hereto."* So accepted Quote IS the contract — no separate `orders` table. Locked: (1) `master_service_agreements` table introduced — per-Client, 12-month term per §2.i, with `signedAt`, `expiresAt`, `signedPdfStorageKey`, `dropboxSignDocumentId`, status enum, `templateVersion`, termination cols (§2.ii); (2) commercial columns move off `campaigns` onto `quotes`; (3) FK direction flips to `campaigns.acceptedQuoteId` so the operational delivery (Event in MSA noun) hangs off the accepted Quote; (4) first-deal e-sig **bundles MSA + first Quote in one Dropbox Sign envelope** (user 2026-05-11 — single envelope with two documents, not merged PDF); (5) NS HST 15% confirmed as seller-side default per §9 governing law (Dartmouth NS — partially resolves 0026's tax OQ). Five phases scaffolded: decision doc + cross-plan reconciliation (edits 0025/0026/0035 plan docs); MSA schema + migration; quotes schema patch into 0026 Phase 2 sketch; drop commercial cols from `campaigns` (gated on 0026 P2 + 0035 P3); tests + wiki sweep. Two related project memories saved: `project_coach_owned_business` (multi-tenant-by-coach: leads/campaigns/quotes coach-owned, dealers/contacts shared registry — drives upstream funnel design) and `project_msa_structure` (the MSA clauses driving the schema).
